</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L202" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="202"></td>
        <td id="LC202" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\section</span>{basic definitions}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L203" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="203"></td>
        <td id="LC203" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L204" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="204"></td>
        <td id="LC204" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L205" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="205"></td>
        <td id="LC205" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{definition}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L206" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="206"></td>
        <td id="LC206" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">A graph <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(V,E)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> has the <span class="pl-c1">\emph</span>{<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-order property} if there exist <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span>, a_k,b_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span>, b_k<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> V<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_ib_j<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> E<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> if and only if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> j<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>. If <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(V,E)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> does not have the <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-order property, then it is <span class="pl-c1">\emph</span>{<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L207" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="207"></td>
        <td id="LC207" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{definition}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L208" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="208"></td>
        <td id="LC208" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L209" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="209"></td>
        <td id="LC209" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Assume <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is an abelian group.  </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L210" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="210"></td>
        <td id="LC210" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{definition}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L211" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="211"></td>
        <td id="LC211" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Given <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, say <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-c1">\emph</span>{<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable} if the graph <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(G,<span class="pl-c1">\{</span>xy: x+y<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> A<span class="pl-cce">\}</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable.  We say <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> <span class="pl-c1">\emph</span>{has the <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-order property} if the graph <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(G,<span class="pl-c1">\{</span>xy: x+y<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> A<span class="pl-cce">\}</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> has the <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-order property.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L212" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="212"></td>
        <td id="LC212" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{definition}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L213" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="213"></td>
        <td id="LC213" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L214" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="214"></td>
        <td id="LC214" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Observe that if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable, then either <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A=G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> or <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A=<span class="pl-c1">\emptyset</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Since this is not interesting, we will throughout restrict to the case where <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>. Given <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, we are interested in understanding the graph <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\Gamma</span>_A:=(G,<span class="pl-c1">\{</span>xy: x+y<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> A<span class="pl-cce">\}</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  In particular our goal is to show that if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\Gamma</span>_A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable, then one can prove a version of Szermeredi&#39;s regularity lemma where the parts have the additional structure of all being approximately translates of a Bohr set of bounded parameters.  We will obtain sharper results when <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is of the form <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{F}_p^n<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> for a fixed prime <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>p<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and large <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>n<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L215" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="215"></td>
        <td id="LC215" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L216" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="216"></td>
        <td id="LC216" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">We now go over some preliminaries. Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a finite abelian group.  Then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\widehat</span>{G}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> denotes the group of characters of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, that is, the set of homomorphisms from <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> into <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{T}=<span class="pl-c1">\{</span>z<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{C}: |z|=<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-cce">\}</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Given <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f:G<span class="pl-c1">\rightarrow</span> <span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{C}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\gamma\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">\widehat</span>{G}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, recall </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L217" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="217"></td>
        <td id="LC217" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L218" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="218"></td>
        <td id="LC218" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-c1">\widehat</span>{f}(<span class="pl-c1">\gamma</span>)=<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{E}_{x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G} f(x)<span class="pl-c1">\gamma</span>(x).</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L219" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="219"></td>
        <td id="LC219" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L220" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="220"></td>
        <td id="LC220" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L221" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="221"></td>
        <td id="LC221" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L222" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="222"></td>
        <td id="LC222" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L223" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="223"></td>
        <td id="LC223" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\section</span>{excellence}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L224" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="224"></td>
        <td id="LC224" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is an abelian group, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A, B<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>y<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Define <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A^{y}_B(x)=(A+y)(x)B(x)=<span class="pl-c1">1</span>_{B<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (A+y)}(x)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>. </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L225" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="225"></td>
        <td id="LC225" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L226" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="226"></td>
        <td id="LC226" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{definition}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L227" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="227"></td>
        <td id="LC227" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A, B<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>y<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  We say <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>y<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-c1">\emph</span>{<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> with respect to <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>} if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\sup</span>_{t<span class="pl-c1">\neq</span> 0}|<span class="pl-c1">\widehat</span>{A_B^{-y}}(t)|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> |B|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L228" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="228"></td>
        <td id="LC228" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{definition}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L229" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="229"></td>
        <td id="LC229" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L230" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="230"></td>
        <td id="LC230" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The set <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> will often be a fixed distinguished set.  In this case, we will just refer to <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>y<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> as <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L231" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="231"></td>
        <td id="LC231" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L232" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="232"></td>
        <td id="LC232" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{definition}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L233" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="233"></td>
        <td id="LC233" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A, B<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  We say <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-c1">\emph</span>{totally <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>} if every <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>y<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> with respect to <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  In other words, if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\widehat</span>{A_B^{-y}}(t)|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>|B|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> for all <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>y<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>t<span class="pl-c1">\neq</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L234" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="234"></td>
        <td id="LC234" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{definition}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L235" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="235"></td>
        <td id="LC235" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L236" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="236"></td>
        <td id="LC236" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The goal of this paper is to show that when <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable for some <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then we can find a totally <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular set <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> with nice structural properties.  In particular, when <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G=<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{F}_p^n<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> will be a subgroup of index bounded by <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>C(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, where <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>C=C(k)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is some constant depending on <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  When <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G=<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{Z}_N<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> will be a Bohr set <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B=B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> where <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|K|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> are bounded in terms of functions of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>. In fact we will prove something even stronger.  </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L237" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="237"></td>
        <td id="LC237" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L238" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="238"></td>
        <td id="LC238" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{definition}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L239" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="239"></td>
        <td id="LC239" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A, B<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>y<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>. Then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>g<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-c1">\emph</span>{<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-good for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>} if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|(A-g)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> |B|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> or <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|B<span class="pl-c1">\setminus</span> (A-g)|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> |B|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>. We say <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-c1">\emph</span>{<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-excellent} if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>y<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-good for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, for all <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>y<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L240" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="240"></td>

</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L242" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="242"></td>
        <td id="LC242" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L243" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="243"></td>
        <td id="LC243" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\section</span>{things we&#39;ll need about Bohr sets}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L244" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="244"></td>
        <td id="LC244" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In this section we state facts and definitions we will need about Bohr sets.  Most of this section come from <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{GW2011} and Tao and Vu.  Assume for this section that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a finite abelian group.  Given <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>K<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\widehat</span>{G}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho\in</span> [<span class="pl-c1">0</span>,<span class="pl-c1">1</span>]<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, define </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L245" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="245"></td>
        <td id="LC245" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L246" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="246"></td>
        <td id="LC246" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s">B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>)=<span class="pl-c1">\{</span>x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G: |<span class="pl-c1">\gamma</span>(x)-<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rho</span> <span class="pl-c1">\text</span>{ for all <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\gamma\in</span> K<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>}<span class="pl-cce">\}</span>.</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L247" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="247"></td>
        <td id="LC247" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L248" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="248"></td>
        <td id="LC248" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">A set of the form <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is called a <span class="pl-c1">\emph</span>{Bohr set}.  Observe a Bohr set is always symmetric (CHECK IT IS TRUE).  Observe that in <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{F}_p^n<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&lt;<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/p<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is the subgroup <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\langle</span> K<span class="pl-c1">\rangle</span> ^{<span class="pl-c1">\perp</span>}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>. We say a Bohr set <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B=B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-c1">\emph</span>{regular} if for all <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> (<span class="pl-c1">0</span>,<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">100</span>|K|)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L249" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="249"></td>
        <td id="LC249" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L250" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="250"></td>
        <td id="LC250" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s">|B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>+<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>))|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> |B|(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>+<span class="pl-c1">100</span>|K|<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>) <span class="pl-c1">\text</span>{ and }|B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>))|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> |B|(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>-<span class="pl-c1">100</span>|K|<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>) </span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L251" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="251"></td>
        <td id="LC251" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L252" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="252"></td>
        <td id="LC252" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L253" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="253"></td>
        <td id="LC253" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{lemma}[Lemma 4.25 in Tao and Vu]<span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{lemma2.1}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L254" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="254"></td>
        <td id="LC254" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Given <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>K<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&gt;<span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, there is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&#39;<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> [<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>, <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>]<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&#39;)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is regular.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L255" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="255"></td>
        <td id="LC255" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{lemma}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L256" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="256"></td>
        <td id="LC256" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L257" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="257"></td>
        <td id="LC257" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{definition}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L258" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="258"></td>
        <td id="LC258" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Given <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&gt;<span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and Bohr sets <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B=B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B&#39;=B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, we write <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B&#39;<span class="pl-c1">\prec</span>_{<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>}B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B&#39;<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> are both regular, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span> <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> [<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>/<span class="pl-c1">400</span>|K|, <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>/<span class="pl-c1">200</span>|K|]<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  We let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B^+=B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span> +<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B^-=B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span> -<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L259" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="259"></td>
        <td id="LC259" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{definition}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L260" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="260"></td>
        <td id="LC260" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L261" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="261"></td>
        <td id="LC261" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Observe that if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B=B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B&#39;=B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B&#39;<span class="pl-c1">\prec</span>_{<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>}B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B&#39;+B<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> B^+<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|(B&#39;+B)<span class="pl-c1">\Delta</span> B^+|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> ?<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L265" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="265"></td>
        <td id="LC265" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Given <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x,y<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{R}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&gt;<span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, we write <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x<span class="pl-c1">\approx</span>_{<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>}y<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> to mean <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|x-y|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  </td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L266" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="266"></td>

        <td id="L267" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="267"></td>
        <td id="LC267" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{lemma}[Lemma 2.3 from <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{GW2011}]</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L268" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="268"></td>
        <td id="LC268" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&gt;<span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B=B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a regular Bohr set.  Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B&#39;=B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\prec</span>_{<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>}B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B^+=B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>+<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>. Then for every function <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f:G<span class="pl-c1">\rightarrow</span> <span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{C}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>||f||_{<span class="pl-c1">\infty</span>}<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> the following holds.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L269" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="269"></td>
        <td id="LC269" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{enumerate}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L270" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="270"></td>
        <td id="LC270" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\item</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{E}_{x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B}f(x) <span class="pl-c1">\approx</span>_{<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>} <span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{E}_{x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B}<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{E}_{y<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> P} f(x+y)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> for every subset <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>P<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> B&#39;<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>. <span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{lemmapart1}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L271" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="271"></td>

        <td id="L276" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="276"></td>
        <td id="LC276" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">We prove (<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{lemmapart2}).  By definition, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> B^{+}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, thus <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|B|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> |B^+|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span>&lt;<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span> &lt;<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>/<span class="pl-c1">200</span>|K|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is regular, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|B^+|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> (<span class="pl-c1">1</span>+<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> /<span class="pl-c1">2</span>)|B|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Now observe</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L277" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="277"></td>

        <td id="LC278" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\Big</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{E}_{x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B^+}f(x) -<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{E}_{x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B}f(x)<span class="pl-c1">\Big</span>|&amp;=<span class="pl-c1">\Big</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{1}{|B^+|}<span class="pl-c1">\sum</span>_{x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B^+<span class="pl-c1">\setminus</span> B}f(x) +<span class="pl-c1">\Big</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{1}{|B^+|}-<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{1}{|B|}<span class="pl-c1">\Big</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\sum</span>_{x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B}f(x)<span class="pl-c1">\Big</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\\</span></td>

      </tr>

        <td id="LC289" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">If <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G=<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{F}_p^n<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> then in the above we can take <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> small so that equalities all hold.</td>

        <td id="L292" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="292"></td>
        <td id="LC292" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\section</span>{regular pairs}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L293" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="293"></td>
        <td id="LC293" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L294" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="294"></td>
        <td id="LC294" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">We begin with a lemma which says regular pairs in stable graphs must have density close to <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> or <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>. Given a graph <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G=(V,E)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> V<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>N(x)=<span class="pl-c1">\{</span>v<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> V: xv<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> E<span class="pl-cce">\}</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d(x)=|N(x)|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  If <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>Y<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> V<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d_Y(x)=|N(x)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> Y|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\neg</span> Y=V<span class="pl-c1">\setminus</span> Y<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  We will use the following.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L295" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="295"></td>
        <td id="LC295" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L296" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="296"></td>
        <td id="LC296" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{fact}<span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{fact0}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L297" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="297"></td>
        <td id="LC297" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is an integer. If <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&lt;(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">2</span>)^k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{1}{k}}-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&gt;<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{2}{k}}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L298" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="298"></td>
        <td id="LC298" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{fact}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L299" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="299"></td>
        <td id="LC299" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{proof}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L300" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="300"></td>
        <td id="LC300" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Set <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>=<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/k}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&lt;(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">2</span>)^k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>&lt;<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  We want to show <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span> -<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>^k <span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>^<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  This is equivalent to showing <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span> -<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>^<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>^k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>&lt;<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, we have <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>&gt;<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>^<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, which implies <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span> -<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>^<span class="pl-c1">2</span>&gt;<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>^<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>. Since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, we thus have <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span> -<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>^<span class="pl-c1">2</span>&gt;<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>^<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>^k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L301" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="301"></td>
        <td id="LC301" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{proof}</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L302" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="302"></td>
        <td id="LC302" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L303" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="303"></td>
        <td id="LC303" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{lemma}<span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{lemma1}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L304" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="304"></td>
        <td id="LC304" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For all <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>t<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span>&lt;<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&lt;(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">2</span>)^{2t+2}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, there is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>m=m(t,<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that the following holds.  Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G=(V,E)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>t<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable graph and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>X, Y<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> V<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> satisfy that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|X|=|Y|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> m<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(X,Y)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular.  Then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d(X,Y)<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{1}{2t+2}}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> or <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d(X,Y)<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{1}{2t+2}}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L305" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="305"></td>
        <td id="LC305" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{lemma}</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L306" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="306"></td>
        <td id="LC306" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{proof}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L307" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="307"></td>
        <td id="LC307" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k=<span class="pl-c1">2</span>t+<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Fix <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>m&gt;k/<span class="pl-c1">2</span>-<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> sufficiently large so that for all <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>n<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> m<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/k}-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>)n-<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{2/k}n<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and for all <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>n<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{2(t-1)/k}m<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>n-<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> m<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Such an <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>m<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> exists because of Fact <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{fact0}. Suppose towards a contradiction <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>X, Y<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> V<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> satisfy that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|X|=|Y|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> m<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(X,Y)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular, and that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{1}{k}} &lt; d(X,Y)&lt; <span class="pl-c1">1</span>-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{1}{k}}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  We build by induction a sequence <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span>, x_t,y_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span>, y_t<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> that is a half-graph.</td>
      </tr>

</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L309" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="309"></td>
        <td id="LC309" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d(X,Y)&gt;<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{1}{k}}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, there is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x_<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\in</span> X<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d_Y(x)<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{1}{k}} |Y|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>Y_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>=N(x)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> Y<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>Z=X<span class="pl-c1">\setminus</span> <span class="pl-c1">\{</span>x_<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-cce">\}</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Because <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>m<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is large, because <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&lt;<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/4}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and by definition of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>Z,Y_<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, we have that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|Y_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>|Y|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|Z|=|X|-<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> |X|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Thus since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(X,Y)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular, </td>
      </tr>

        <td id="LC322" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Since (1) holds and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(X,Y)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular, we have that </td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L328" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="328"></td>
        <td id="LC328" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s">|N(x_{i+1})<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> Y_i|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> (<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/k}-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>)|Y_i|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> (<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/k}-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{(2i-1)/k}|Y|&gt;(<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{2/k})<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{(2i-1)/k}|Y|=<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{(2(i+1)-1)/k}|Y|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> |Y|,</span></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L330" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="330"></td>
        <td id="LC330" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">where the second to last inequality is by Fact <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{fact0}, and the last inequality is because <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i&lt;t<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> implies <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2</span>(i+<span class="pl-c1">1</span>)-<span class="pl-c1">1</span>)/k<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>. Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>Y_{i+1}=N(x_{i+1})<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> Y_i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>Z=X_i<span class="pl-c1">\setminus</span> <span class="pl-c1">\{</span>x_{i+1}<span class="pl-cce">\}</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Note <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|Z|=|X_{i}|-<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{2i/k}|X|-<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> |X|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> because of our choice of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>m<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and because <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{2i/k}<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{2(t-1)/k}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> (since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i&lt;t<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>).  Thus, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|Z|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> |X|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|Y_{i+1}|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> |Y|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, so by <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regularity of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(X,Y)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, we have</td>

        <td id="L331" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="331"></td>

        <td id="LC332" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s">d(Z,Y_{i+1})<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> d(X,Y)+<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> &lt; <span class="pl-c1">1</span>-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/k}+<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>.</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L333" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="333"></td>
        <td id="LC333" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L334" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="334"></td>
        <td id="LC334" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Thus there is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>y_{i+1}<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> Y_{i+1}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|Z<span class="pl-c1">\setminus</span> N(y_{i+1})|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> (<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/k}-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>)|Z|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Set <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>X_{i+1}=Z<span class="pl-c1">\setminus</span> N(y_{i+1})<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  By definition of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>X_{i+1}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and our induction hypothesis we have</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L335" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="335"></td>
        <td id="LC335" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{align*}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L336" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="336"></td>
        <td id="LC336" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">|X_{i+1}|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> (<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/k}-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>)|Z|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> (<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/k}-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>)(|X_i|-1)<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> (<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/k}-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>)(<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{2i/k}|X|-1)&amp;<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{2/k}(<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{2i/k}|X|)<span class="pl-c1">\\</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L337" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="337"></td>
        <td id="LC337" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">&amp;=<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{2(i+1)/k}|X|,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L338" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="338"></td>
        <td id="LC338" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{align*}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L339" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="339"></td>
        <td id="LC339" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">where the last inequality is because of our assumption on <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>m<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and because <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{2(i+1)/k}|X|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> m<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> (since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i+<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> t<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> imples <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span>(i+<span class="pl-c1">1</span>)/k<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>).  This finishes the inductive step of our construction.  At the end we have built <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span>, x_t, y_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span>, y_t<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x_iy_j<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> E<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> if and only if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> j<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, contradicting that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>t<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable.  </td>
      </tr>

        <td id="LC342" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">We now prove a lemma which allows us to move between the graph and group setting.         <td id="LC345" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a finite abelian group and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>U,V,W<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> are functions from <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> to <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{C}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.       <tr>
        <td id="L357" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="357"></td>
        <td id="LC357" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Now recall that if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>t+u+v<span class="pl-c1">\neq</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\sum</span>_{<span class="pl-c1">\gamma</span> <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">\widehat</span>{G}}<span class="pl-c1">\gamma</span>(t+u+v) =<span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>t+u+v=<span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\sum</span>_{<span class="pl-c1">\gamma</span> <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">\widehat</span>{G}}<span class="pl-c1">\gamma</span>(t+u+v)=|G|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.       </tr>

        <td id="L364" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="364"></td>
        <td id="LC364" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{fact}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L365" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="365"></td>
        <td id="LC365" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B=B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a Bohr set.  Then </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L366" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="366"></td>
        <td id="LC366" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L367" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="367"></td>
        <td id="LC367" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{|A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B|}{|B|}=<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{|(-A)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B|}{|B|}.</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L368" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="368"></td>
        <td id="LC368" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L369" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="369"></td>
        <td id="LC369" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{fact}</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L370" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="370"></td>
        <td id="LC370" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{proof}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L371" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="371"></td>
        <td id="LC371" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a Bohr set, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is symmetric.  Thus the map <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>h<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> which sends <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> to <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>-a<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a map from <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> to <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(-A)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Clearly this map in injective.  We show it is surjective.  Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>-a<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> (-A)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>. Then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is symmetric, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>-a<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> implies <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.   Thus <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and we are done.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L372" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="372"></td>
        <td id="LC372" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{proof}</td>
      </tr>

</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L374" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="374"></td>
        <td id="LC374" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L375" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="375"></td>
        <td id="LC375" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{lemma}[new version]<span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{reg}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L376" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="376"></td>
        <td id="LC376" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is an abelian group, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&gt;<span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>y<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B&#39;<span class="pl-c1">\prec</span>_{<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^2} B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> are Bohr sets.  Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span> = |(A-y)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B|/|B|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and suppose that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f(x)=(-A)^{+y}_B(x)<span class="pl-c1">\mu</span>_B(x)-<span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span> <span class="pl-c1">\mu</span>_B(x)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> satisfies <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\sup</span>_{t<span class="pl-c1">\neq</span> 0}|<span class="pl-c1">\widehat</span>{f}(t)|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(B&#39;,B+y)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is an <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular pair in <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\Gamma</span>_A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|d(B&#39;,B+y)-<span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>. </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L377" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="377"></td>
        <td id="LC377" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{lemma}</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L378" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="378"></td>
        <td id="LC378" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{proof}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L379" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="379"></td>
        <td id="LC379" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Throughout, we will use <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B^+<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> as in Definition ? in case 2, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B^+=B=B&#39;<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> in case 1, so that in both cases, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B&#39;+B<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> B^+<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  We first show the assertions concerning <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d(B&#39;,B+y)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Observe</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L380" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="380"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L381" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="381"></td>
        <td id="LC381" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">|d(B&#39;,B+y)|&amp;=<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{<span class="pl-c1">\sum</span>_{b&#39;<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B&#39;} |N(b&#39;)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (B+y)|}{|B||B&#39;|}=<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{<span class="pl-c1">\sum</span>_{b&#39;<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B&#39;} |B<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (A-y-b&#39;)|}{|B||B&#39;|}<span class="pl-c1">\\</span></td>
      </tr>

We now prove the assertions concerning the regularity of the pair <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(B&#39;,B+y)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>U<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> B&#39;<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>V<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> satisfy <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|U|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>}|B&#39;|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|V|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>}|B|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  By what we have already shown, </td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L385" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="385"></td>

        <td id="LC386" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">|d(U,V+g)-d(B&#39;,B+g)|&amp;=|d(U,V+g)-<span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>+<span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>-d(B&#39;,B+g)|<span class="pl-c1">\\</span></td>

        <td id="LC389" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Therefore, it suffices to show <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|d(U,V+g)-<span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>. Note that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f(x)=h(x)<span class="pl-c1">\mu</span>_B(x)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Note</td>

        <td id="LC391" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">d(U,V+g)&amp;=<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{1}{|U||V|}<span class="pl-c1">\sum</span>_{u,v<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G}A^{-g}(u+v)U(u)V(v)=<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{1}{|U||V|}<span class="pl-c1">\sum</span>_{u,v<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G}A_{B^+}^{-g}(u+v)U(u)V(v).</td>

        <td id="L406" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="406"></td>
        <td id="LC406" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">where the last equality is by Claim <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{claim}.         <td id="L408" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="408"></td>
        <td id="LC408" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{|G|^2}{|U||V|}|<span class="pl-c1">\widehat</span>{h}(<span class="pl-c1">\mathbf</span>{1})<span class="pl-c1">\widehat</span>{U}(<span class="pl-c1">\mathbf</span>{1})<span class="pl-c1">\widehat</span>{V}(<span class="pl-c1">\mathbf</span>{1})|&amp;=<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{|G|^2}{|U||V|}<span class="pl-c1">\Big</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\Big</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{1}{|G|}<span class="pl-c1">\sum</span>_{x <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G}((-A)_{B^+}^{+y}-<span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span> B^{+})(x)<span class="pl-c1">\Big</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\Big</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{1}{|G|}<span class="pl-c1">\sum</span>_{x <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G}U(x)<span class="pl-c1">\Big</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\Big</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{1}{|G|}<span class="pl-c1">\sum</span>_{x <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G}V(x)<span class="pl-c1">\Big</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\Big</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\\</span></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L411" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="411"></td>
        <td id="LC411" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{align*}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L412" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="412"></td>
        <td id="LC412" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Note <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{|(A-y)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B^{+}|}{|B^+|}=<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{E}_{x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B^+}(A-y)(x)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>=<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{E}_{x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B}(A-y)(x)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Thus by Lemma <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{lemma2.3} part (1), and the above, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{|G|^2}{|U||V|}|<span class="pl-c1">\widehat</span>{h}(<span class="pl-c1">\mathbf</span>{1})<span class="pl-c1">\widehat</span>{U}(<span class="pl-c1">\mathbf</span>{1})<span class="pl-c1">\widehat</span>{V}(<span class="pl-c1">\mathbf</span>{1})|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> |<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{|(A-y)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B^{+}|}{|B^+|}-<span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.       <tr>
        <td id="L446" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="446"></td>
        <td id="LC446" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&lt;(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">2</span>)^{4k+4}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a finite abelian group, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable. If <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>y<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f=((-A)^{+y}_B-<span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\mu</span>_B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>y<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+2)}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-good for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>

        <td id="LC450" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>g=<span class="pl-c1">1</span>_H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> in case 1 and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>g=f<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> in case 2.       <tr>
        <td id="L452" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="452"></td>
        <td id="LC452" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+2)}|Z|&lt;|(A-y)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> Z|&lt;(1-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+2)})|Z|.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L453" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="453"></td>
        <td id="LC453" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{align}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L454" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="454"></td>
        <td id="LC454" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In case 1, by Lemma <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{reg} and (<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{p}), <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(Z&#39;,Z+y)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular in <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\Gamma</span>_A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+k)}-error&lt;d(Z,Z&#39;+y)&lt;(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+2)})+error<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  By assumption, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|Z|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> |Z&#39;|=|Z&#39;+y|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span>  m(k,<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Also by assumption, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>}&lt;(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">2</span>)^{2k+2}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>}^{1/(2k+2)}=<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+k)}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, Lemma <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{lemma1} implies <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d(Z,Z&#39;+g)<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+k)}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> or <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d(H,H+g)<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+k)}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, a contradiction. Consequently, either <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+2)}|Z|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> |(A-y)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> Z|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, in which case ... or <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|(A-y)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> Z|&lt;(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+2)})|Z|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, in which case...</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L455" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="455"></td>
        <td id="LC455" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{proof}</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L458" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="458"></td>
        <td id="LC458" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In cases where <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{F}_p^n<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, we can take <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>=<span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> so that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B=B&#39;<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a subgroup.</td>
