      <tr>
        <td id="L462" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="462"></td>
        <td id="LC462" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\section</span>{Key Lemma: dense stable sets contain most of a translate of Bohr set}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L463" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="463"></td>
        <td id="LC463" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L464" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="464"></td>
        <td id="LC464" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In this section we prove a key lemma, Proposition <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{keylem}, which shows that a dense set which is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable has to contain most of a coset of a subgroup with index bounded by <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>C(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> for some constant <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>C<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> depending on <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>. We begin with some observations.  Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>||x||<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> denote the distance from <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> to the nearest integer.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L465" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="465"></td>
        <td id="LC465" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L466" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="466"></td>
        <td id="LC466" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L467" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="467"></td>
        <td id="LC467" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{observation}<span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{lemma11}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L468" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="468"></td>
        <td id="LC468" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B=B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a regular Bohr set, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>=|(A-y)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B|/|B|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f=((-A)_B^{+y}-<span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\mu</span>_B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\beta</span>=|B|/|G|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  If <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>y<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is not <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then there is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span> <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> [<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rho</span> /<span class="pl-c1">400</span>|K|, <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>/<span class="pl-c1">200</span>|K|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>t<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-c1">\setminus</span> K<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that for some <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B&#39;&#39;=B(K<span class="pl-c1">\cup</span> <span class="pl-c1">\{</span>t<span class="pl-cce">\}</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&#39;)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B&#39;&#39;<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is regular and</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L469" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="469"></td>
        <td id="LC469" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{align}<span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{align}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L470" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="470"></td>
        <td id="LC470" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{|(A-y)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (B&#39;&#39;+x)|}{|B&#39;&#39;|}<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>+<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>}{2}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L471" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="471"></td>
        <td id="LC471" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{align}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L472" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="472"></td>
        <td id="LC472" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{observation}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L473" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="473"></td>
        <td id="LC473" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{proof}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L474" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="474"></td>
        <td id="LC474" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>y<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is not <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, there is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>t<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\widehat</span>{f}(t)|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>K&#39;=K<span class="pl-c1">\cup</span> <span class="pl-c1">\{</span>t<span class="pl-cce">\}</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>g(x)=(-A)^{+y}(x)<span class="pl-c1">\mu</span>_B(x)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> so <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f(x)=g(x)-<span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span> <span class="pl-c1">\mu</span>_B(x)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Observe the following.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L475" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="475"></td>
        <td id="LC475" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{align*}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L476" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="476"></td>
        <td id="LC476" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\hat</span>{f}(t)=<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{E}_{x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G}f(x) <span class="pl-c1">\omega</span>^{xt}=<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{E}_{x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G}(g(x)-<span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span> <span class="pl-c1">\mu</span>_B(x))<span class="pl-c1">\omega</span>^{xt}=<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{E}_{x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B}((-A)^{+y}(x)-<span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\omega</span>^{xt}=<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{E}_{x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B}(<span class="pl-c1">\beta</span> g(x)-<span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\omega</span>^{xt}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L477" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="477"></td>
        <td id="LC477" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{align*}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L478" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="478"></td>
        <td id="LC478" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Now let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B&#39;<span class="pl-c1">\prec</span>_{<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>/16} B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, for some <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B&#39;=B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&#39;)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> where <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&#39; <span class="pl-c1">\in</span>  [<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rho</span> /(<span class="pl-c1">16</span>)<span class="pl-c1">400</span>|K|, <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>/(<span class="pl-c1">16</span>)<span class="pl-c1">200</span>|K|]<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> (which exists by the remark following Lemma <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{lemma2.1}).  Find <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&#39;&#39;<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> [<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&#39;/<span class="pl-c1">2</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&#39;]<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> so that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B&#39;&#39;=B(K<span class="pl-c1">\cup</span> <span class="pl-c1">\{</span>t<span class="pl-cce">\}</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&#39;&#39;)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is regular (note <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&#39;&#39;<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> [<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rho</span> /<span class="pl-c1">16</span>(<span class="pl-c1">400</span>)|K|, <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>/<span class="pl-c1">1600</span>|K|]<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>).  Note <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B&#39;&#39;<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> B&#39;<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  By Lemma <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{?} part (<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{lemmapart1}), since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B&#39;&#39;<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> B&#39;<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, we have the following.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L479" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="479"></td>
        <td id="LC479" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{align*}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L480" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="480"></td>
        <td id="LC480" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\hat</span>{f}(t)=<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{E}_{x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B}(<span class="pl-c1">\beta</span> g(x)-<span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\omega</span>^{xt}<span class="pl-c1">\approx</span>_{<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>/16}&amp;<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{E}_{x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B}<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{E}_{z<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B&#39;&#39;} (<span class="pl-c1">\beta</span> g(x+z)-<span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\omega</span>^{(x+z)t}<span class="pl-c1">\\</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L481" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="481"></td>
        <td id="LC481" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">=&amp;<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{E}_{x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B}<span class="pl-c1">\omega</span>^{xt}<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{E}_{z<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B&#39;&#39;}(<span class="pl-c1">\beta</span> g(x+z)-<span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\omega</span>^{zt}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L482" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="482"></td>
        <td id="LC482" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{align*}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L483" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="483"></td>
        <td id="LC483" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Note that for all <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>z<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B&#39;&#39;<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, by definition, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>-<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&#39;&#39; <span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> ||zt/N|| <span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&#39;&#39;<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Consequently, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\omega</span>^{zt}-<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|=|<span class="pl-c1">\sin</span> (||zt/N||)|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>||zt/N||&lt;<span class="pl-c1">\pi</span>/<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\sin</span> (||zt/N||)|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> | ||zt/N|| |<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&#39;&#39;<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Thus for each <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>z<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B&#39;&#39;<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\omega</span>^{zt}<span class="pl-c1">\approx</span>_{<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&#39;&#39;}<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Consequently, since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&#39;&#39;&lt;<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>/<span class="pl-c1">16</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L484" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="484"></td>
        <td id="LC484" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{align*}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L485" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="485"></td>

        <td id="LC527" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>+5<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>/16 <span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\beta</span> g<span class="pl-c1">\ast</span> <span class="pl-c1">\mu</span>_{B&#39;&#39;}(x)&amp;=<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{1}{|G|}<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{|G|}{|B&#39;&#39;|}<span class="pl-c1">\sum</span>_{z<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G}<span class="pl-c1">\beta</span> g(z)B&#39;&#39;(x-z)<span class="pl-c1">\\</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L528" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="528"></td>
        <td id="LC528" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">&amp;=<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{|B|}{|G|} <span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{|(-A)^{+y}<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (B&#39;&#39;+x)|}{|B&#39;&#39;|}<span class="pl-c1">\\</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L529" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="529"></td>
        <td id="LC529" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">&amp;<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span>  <span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{|(-A)^{+y}<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (B&#39;&#39;+x)|}{|B&#39;&#39;|}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L530" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="530"></td>
        <td id="LC530" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{align*}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L531" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="531"></td>
        <td id="LC531" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Now we need to argue that because <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B&#39;&#39;+x<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is basically contained in <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, so that this is essentially telling us </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L532" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="532"></td>
        <td id="LC532" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L533" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="533"></td>
        <td id="LC533" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>+<span class="pl-c1">4</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>/<span class="pl-c1">8</span><span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{|(-A)^{+y}<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (B&#39;&#39;+x)|}{|B&#39;&#39;|}=<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{|(-A)^{+y-x}<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span>  B&#39;&#39;|}{|B&#39;&#39;|}=<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{|A^{-y+x}<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span>  B&#39;&#39;|}{|B&#39;&#39;|},</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L534" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="534"></td>
        <td id="LC534" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L535" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="535"></td>
        <td id="LC535" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">where the last equality is because <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B&#39;&#39;<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a Bohr set and is thus symmetric.</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L540" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="540"></td>
        <td id="LC540" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{lemma}<span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{incrementlem}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L541" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="541"></td>
        <td id="LC541" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&gt;<span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a sufficiently large finite abelian group and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B=B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a regular Bohr set.  Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>:= <span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{|A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B|}{|B|}<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Then there is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>K_<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\supseteq</span> K<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>y<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|K_<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\setminus</span> K|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> ??<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>_<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\in</span> [?,?]<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> so that if such that if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>=B(K_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is regular, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>y<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (A+g)|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span> |B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L544" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="544"></td>
        <td id="LC544" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose first we are in situation 1. Fix any <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>g_<span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  If <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>g_<span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H_<span class="pl-c1">0</span>=H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then we are done, since </td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L545" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="545"></td>
        <td id="LC545" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L546" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="546"></td>
        <td id="LC546" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s">|(A+g_<span class="pl-c1">0</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> H_<span class="pl-c1">0</span>|=|(A+g_<span class="pl-c1">0</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> H|=<span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span> |H|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> |H|=<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> |H_<span class="pl-c1">0</span>|.</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L547" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="547"></td>
        <td id="LC547" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L548" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="548"></td>
        <td id="LC548" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose now that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>g_<span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is not <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H_<span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Assume <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and suppose by induction we have constructed a sequence of subgroups <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H_<span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span> <span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> H_i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and chosen <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>g_<span class="pl-c1">0</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span>, g_i<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that the following hold.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L549" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="549"></td>
        <td id="LC549" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{enumerate}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L550" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="550"></td>
        <td id="LC550" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\item</span> For each <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> j&lt;i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H_j<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> has index <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>p<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> in <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H_{j+1}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and consequently, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H_i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> has index <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>p^i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> in <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L551" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="551"></td>
        <td id="LC551" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\item</span> For each <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> j<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|(A+g_j)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> H_j|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> (<span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>+<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{j<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>}{2})|H_j|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L552" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="552"></td>
        <td id="LC552" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{enumerate}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L553" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="553"></td>
        <td id="LC553" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">If <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>g_i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H_i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then we are done by our induction hypotheses on <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H_i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>g_i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  So assume <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>g_i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is not <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H_i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Then by Lemma <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{lemma11}, there is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H_{i+1}<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> H_i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> of index <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>p<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and a coset <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x_{i+1}+H_{i+1}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L554" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="554"></td>
        <td id="LC554" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L555" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="555"></td>
        <td id="LC555" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s">|(A+g_i)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (H_{i+1}+x_{i+1})|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\Big</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{|(A+g_i)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> H_i|}{|H_i|}+<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>}{2}<span class="pl-c1">\Big</span>)|H_{i+1}| <span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> (<span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>+<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{i<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>}{2}+<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>}{2})|H_{i+1}|=<span class="pl-c1">\Big</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>+<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{(i+1)<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>}{2}<span class="pl-c1">\Big</span>)|H_{i+1}|,</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L556" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="556"></td>
        <td id="LC556" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L557" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="557"></td>
        <td id="LC557" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">where the second inequality is by our induction hypothesis (2) on $H_i$ and $g_i$.  Let $g_{i+1}=g_i+x_{i+1}$, then we have shown that $|(A+g_{i+1})\cap H_{i+1}|=|(A+g_i)\cap (H_{i+1}+x_{i+1})|\geq (\alpha+ \frac{(i+1)\epsilon}{2})|H_{i+1}|$, and since $H_{i+1}$ has index $p$ in $H_i$, our induction hypothesis (1) for $H_i$ implies $H_{i+1}$ has index $p^{i+1}$ in $G$. This finishes our inductive construction.  Suppose towards a contradiction this went on for $t$ steps, where $t=\lceil \frac{2}{\epsilon}\rceil$.  Then we obtain $H_t$ and $g_t$ such that $|(A+g_t)\cap H_t|\geq \frac{t\epsilon}{2} |H_t|&gt;|H_t|$, a contradiction.  Therefore this process ends at some stage $\ell&lt;\lceil \frac{2}{\epsilon}\rceil$, i.e. $\ell\leq \lfloor \frac{2}{\epsilon}\rfloor\leq \frac{2}{\epsilon}$.  Thus we will obtain $H_{\ell}\leq G$ and $g_{\ell}\in G$ such that $H_{\ell}$ has index at most $p^{\ell}\leq p^{\lfloor 2/\epsilon\rfloor}$, such that $g_{\ell}$ is $\epsilon$-regular for $H_{\ell}$, and $|(A+g_{\ell})\cap H_{\ell}|\geq (\alpha+\frac{\ell \epsilon}{2}) |H_{\ell}|\geq \alpha|H_{\ell}|$.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L558" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="558"></td>
        <td id="LC558" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{proof}</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L559" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="559"></td>
        <td id="LC559" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L560" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="560"></td>
        <td id="LC560" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L561" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="561"></td>
        <td id="LC561" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{proposition}<span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{keylem}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L562" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="562"></td>
        <td id="LC562" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span>&lt;<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&lt;(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">2</span>)^{4k+4}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a finite abelian group, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|A|&gt;<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+4)}|G|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B=B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a Bohr set and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>=<span class="pl-c1">\frac</span>{|A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B|}{|B|}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Then there is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>K_<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\supseteq</span> K<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> with <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|K_<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\setminus</span> K|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> ??<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> so that if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>=B(K_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>+x)|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> (<span class="pl-c1">1</span>-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+4)})|B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L563" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="563"></td>

</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L565" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="565"></td>
        <td id="LC565" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{proof}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L566" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="566"></td>
        <td id="LC566" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>= |A|/|G|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  By our assumption, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>&gt;<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+4)}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Suppose first we are in situation 1. By Lemma <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{incrementlem}, there exists a subgroup <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H_<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> of index at most <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>p^{<span class="pl-c1">\lfloor</span> 2/<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon\rfloor</span> }<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L567" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="567"></td>
        <td id="LC567" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L568" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="568"></td>
        <td id="LC568" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s">|A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (H_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>+x)|=|(A-x)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> H_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>|H_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|&gt;<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+4)}|H_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|.</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L569" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="569"></td>
        <td id="LC569" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L570" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="570"></td>
        <td id="LC570" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">By Proposition <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{goodlem}, because <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&lt;(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">2</span>)^{4k+4}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, either </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L571" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="571"></td>
        <td id="LC571" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L572" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="572"></td>
        <td id="LC572" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s">|(A-x)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> H_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+4)}|H_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\text</span>{ or }|H_<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\setminus</span> (A-x)|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+2)}|H_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|.</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L573" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="573"></td>
        <td id="LC573" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L574" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="574"></td>
        <td id="LC574" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|(A-x)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> H_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>| &gt;<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+4)}|H_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, we must have <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|H_<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\setminus</span> (A-x)|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+4)}|H_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and consequently, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|(A-x)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> H_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> (<span class="pl-c1">1</span>-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+4)})|H_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|(A-x)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> H_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|=|A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (H_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>+x)|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, we are done.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L575" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="575"></td>
        <td id="LC575" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>

</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L577" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="577"></td>
        <td id="LC577" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose now we are in situation 2. By Lemma <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{incrementlem}, there is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>K_<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\supseteq</span> K<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> with <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|K_<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\setminus</span> K|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> ??<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> so that if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>=B(K_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L578" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="578"></td>
        <td id="LC578" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L579" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="579"></td>
        <td id="LC579" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s">|A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>+x)|=|(A-x)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\alpha</span>|B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|&gt;<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+4)}|B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|.</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L580" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="580"></td>
        <td id="LC580" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L581" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="581"></td>
        <td id="LC581" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">By Proposition <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{goodlem}, because <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-regular, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&lt;(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">2</span>)^{4k+4}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, either </td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L582" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="582"></td>
        <td id="LC582" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L583" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="583"></td>
        <td id="LC583" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s">|(A-x)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+4)}|B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\text</span>{ or }|H<span class="pl-c1">\setminus</span> (A-x)|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+2)}|B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|.</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L584" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="584"></td>
        <td id="LC584" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L585" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="585"></td>
        <td id="LC585" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|(A-x)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>| &gt;<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+4)}|B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, we must have <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\setminus</span> (A-x)|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+4)}|B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and consequently, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|(A-x)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> (<span class="pl-c1">1</span>-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+4)})|B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|(A-x)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|=|A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (B_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>+x)|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, we are done.</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="LC590" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\section</span>{Proof of Main Theorem}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L591" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="591"></td>
        <td id="LC591" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is an abelian group. For convenience, if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\Gamma</span>_A=(G,E)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L592" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="592"></td>
        <td id="LC592" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{align*}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L593" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="593"></td>
        <td id="LC593" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">N^1(x)&amp;=N(x)=<span class="pl-cce">\{</span>z<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G: xz<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> E<span class="pl-cce">\}</span><span class="pl-c1">\\</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L594" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="594"></td>
        <td id="LC594" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">N^0(x)&amp;=<span class="pl-c1">\neg</span> N(x)=<span class="pl-cce">\{</span>z<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G: xz<span class="pl-c1">\notin</span> E<span class="pl-cce">\}</span><span class="pl-c1">\\</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L595" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="595"></td>
        <td id="LC595" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">A^1&amp;=A<span class="pl-c1">\\</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L596" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="596"></td>
        <td id="LC596" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">A^0&amp;=<span class="pl-c1">\neg</span> A=G<span class="pl-c1">\setminus</span> A.</td>
      </tr>

      <tr>
        <td id="L599" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="599"></td>
        <td id="LC599" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">We will use the following observations throughout this section.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L600" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="600"></td>
        <td id="LC600" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{observation}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L601" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="601"></td>
        <td id="LC601" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>g, h<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Then in <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\Gamma</span>_A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>N(g)=A-g<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\neg</span> N(g)=<span class="pl-c1">\neg</span> A-g<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>h+N(g)=N(g-h)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>h+<span class="pl-c1">\neg</span> N(g)=<span class="pl-c1">\neg</span> N(g-h)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L602" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="602"></td>

</td>

        <td id="L604" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="604"></td>
        <td id="LC604" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">We now state a few facts we will need.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L605" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="605"></td>
        <td id="LC605" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L606" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="606"></td>
        <td id="LC606" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{fact}<span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{stillstable}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L607" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="607"></td>
        <td id="LC607" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>g,h<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L608" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="608"></td>
        <td id="LC608" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{enumerate}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L609" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="609"></td>
        <td id="LC609" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\item</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A+g<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\neg</span> A+g<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> are <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable in <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L610" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="610"></td>
        <td id="LC610" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\item</span> If <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable in <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L611" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="611"></td>
        <td id="LC611" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{enumerate}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L612" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="612"></td>
        <td id="LC612" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{fact}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L613" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="613"></td>
        <td id="LC613" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{proof}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L614" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="614"></td>
        <td id="LC614" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A+g<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is not <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable.  Then there are <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span>, a_k,b_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span>, b_k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_i+b_j<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> A+g<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> if and only if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> j<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  This implies <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_i-g+b_j<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> if and only if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> j<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a&#39;_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>=a_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>-g,<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span>, a&#39;_k=a_k-g<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>b&#39;_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>=b_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span>, b_k&#39;=b_k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Then we have shown <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a&#39;_i+b_j&#39;<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> if and only if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> j<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, contradicting that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable.  Thus <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A+g<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable.  Clearly <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\neg</span> A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable because <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is.  Thus the same argument as above implies <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\neg</span> A+g<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L615" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="615"></td>
        <td id="LC615" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L616" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="616"></td>
        <td id="LC616" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> but <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is not <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable in <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Then there are <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span>, a_k,b_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span>, b_k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> in <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_i+b_j<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> if and only if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> j<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Note <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> j<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> implies <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_i+b_j<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> H<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  So in order for this to not contradict the fact that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable in <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, we must have that for some <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i&gt;j<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_i+b_j<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  However, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_i,b_j<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> implies <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_i+b_j<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, thus <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_i+b_j<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, contradicting our assumption that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_i+b_j<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> if and only if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> j<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>. Thus <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable in <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>

      <tr>
        <td id="L620" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="620"></td>
        <td id="LC620" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f(x)=<span class="pl-c1">2</span>x<span class="pl-c1">2</span>^x<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  If <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A,B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> are <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable subsets of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f(k)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable.</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L626" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="626"></td>
        <td id="LC626" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Given <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f^i(x)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> denotes the function we obtain by composing <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> with itself <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> times. By convention, let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f^<span class="pl-c1">0</span>(x)=x<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> for all <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L627" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="627"></td>
        <td id="LC627" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L628" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="628"></td>
        <td id="LC628" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Notational conventions: Given an integer <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>n<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, define <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span>^n=<span class="pl-c1">\{</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span>,<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\}</span>^n<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L629" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="629"></td>
        <td id="LC629" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{align*}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L630" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="630"></td>
        <td id="LC630" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">2^{&lt;n}=<span class="pl-c1">\bigcup</span>_{i=0}^{n-1} <span class="pl-cce">\{</span>0,1<span class="pl-cce">\}</span>^i,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L631" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="631"></td>
        <td id="LC631" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{align*}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L632" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="632"></td>
        <td id="LC632" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">where <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\{</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span>,<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\}</span>^<span class="pl-c1">0</span>=<span class="pl-c1">\langle</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rangle</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is the <span class="pl-c1">\emph</span>{empty string}, and for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i&gt;<span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\{</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span>,<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\}</span>^i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is the usual cartesian product.  Given <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>, <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>&#39;<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>^{&lt;n}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, define <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span> <span class="pl-c1">\trianglelefteq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>&#39;<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> if and only if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>=<span class="pl-c1">\langle</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rangle</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> or <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is an initial segment of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>&#39;<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  We will write <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span> <span class="pl-c1">\triangleleft</span> <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>&#39;<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> to denote that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span> <span class="pl-c1">\trianglelefteq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>&#39;<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span> <span class="pl-c1">\neq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>&#39;<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Given <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span> <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">\{</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span>,<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\}</span>^i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>|=i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> denote <span class="pl-c1">\emph</span>{length} of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> (the length of the empty string <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\langle</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rangle</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>). Given <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span> <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>^n<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">\{</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span>,<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-cce">\}</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta\wedge</span> i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> denotes the element of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span>^{n+1}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> obtained by adding <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> to the end of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  If <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>=(<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span>, <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>_n) <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>^n<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> i<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> n<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span> |_i=(<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span>, <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>_i)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>(i)=<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>_i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  By convention, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>|_<span class="pl-c1">0</span>=<span class="pl-c1">\langle</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rangle</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  </td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L635" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="635"></td>
        <td id="LC635" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{definition}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L636" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="636"></td>
        <td id="LC636" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Given a graph <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G=(V,E)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, the <span class="pl-c1">\emph</span>{tree bound} for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is the smallest integer <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d=d(G)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that there does not exist sequences <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\langle</span> a_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}: <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span> <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>^d<span class="pl-c1">\rangle</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\langle</span> b_{<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>}: <span class="pl-c1">\rho</span> <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>^{&lt;d}<span class="pl-c1">\rangle</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, of elements of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>V<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> with the property that for each <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>^d<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>^{&lt;d}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span> <span class="pl-c1">\triangleleft</span> <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}b_{<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>}<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> E<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> if and only if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho\wedge</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\trianglelefteq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L640" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="640"></td>
        <td id="LC640" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For each integer <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, there is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d=d(k)&lt;<span class="pl-c1">2</span>^{k+2}-<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable graph, then the tree bound of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d(G)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, is at most <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L644" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="644"></td>
        <td id="LC644" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is an integer.  If <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span>&lt;<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&lt;(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">2</span>)^{20(k+1)}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(5k+5)}-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+4)}&gt; <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+4)}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>

        <td id="L647" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="647"></td>
        <td id="LC647" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>=<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(k+1)}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  We want to show <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>^{1/5}-<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>^{1/5}&gt;<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>^{1/5}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  This holds if and only if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>^{1/5}&gt;<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>^{1/4}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, which holds if and only if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>^<span class="pl-c1">4</span>&gt;<span class="pl-c1">2</span>^{20}<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>^<span class="pl-c1">5</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, which holds because our choice of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and the definitoin of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> implies <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">2</span>)^{20}&gt;<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L651" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="651"></td>
        <td id="LC651" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For all <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\mu\in</span> (<span class="pl-c1">0</span>,<span class="pl-c1">1</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>,  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, the following holds. </td>

        <td id="L653" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="653"></td>
        <td id="LC653" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\item</span> For a fixed prime <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>p<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and sufficiently large <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>n<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> the following holds.       <tr>
        <td id="L654" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="654"></td>
        <td id="LC654" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\item</span> For sufficiently large prime integers <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>N<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, the following holds. Then there is regular Bohr set <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B=B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span> <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> [?,?]<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|K|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> ?^{d<span class="pl-c1">\lfloor</span> 2/<span class="pl-c1">\mu</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rfloor</span>}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> which is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\mu</span>^{1/(5K+5)}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-excellent for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L658" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="658"></td>
        <td id="LC658" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Set <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>=<span class="pl-c1">\min</span><span class="pl-cce">\{</span><span class="pl-c1">\mu</span>, (<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">2</span>)^{4k+4}, (<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">2</span>)^{20(K+1)}<span class="pl-cce">\}</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, so that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\mu</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> satisfy requirements appearing in Fact <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{fact00} and Proposition <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{keylem}.  By definition of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> <span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\mu</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, it suffices to find an <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(5K+5)}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-excellent <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> whose index is at most <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span>^{d<span class="pl-c1">\lfloor</span> 1/<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon\rfloor</span>}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>. We will use throughout that if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> t<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> d<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f^t(k)<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> K<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  If case 1 holds, let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>m=p^{<span class="pl-c1">\lfloor</span> 2/<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rfloor</span>}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  </td>
      </tr>

</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L660" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="660"></td>
        <td id="LC660" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>Z_{&lt;&gt;}=G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  If <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>Z_{&lt;&gt;}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(5K+5)}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-excellent, then we are done.  So assume <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>Z_{<span class="pl-c1">\langle</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rangle</span>}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is not <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(5K+5)}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-excellent.  This means there exists <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>g_{&lt;&gt;}<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> Z_{&lt;&gt;}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that</td>

        <td id="L661" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="661"></td>

        <td id="LC662" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">&amp;|N(g_{&lt;&gt;})<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> Z_{&lt;&gt;}|=|(A-g_{&lt;&gt;})<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> Z_{&lt;&gt;}|&gt; <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(5K+5)} |Z_{&lt;&gt;}|<span class="pl-c1">\text</span>{ and }<span class="pl-c1">\\</span></td>
