        <td id="L665" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="665"></td>
        <td id="LC665" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Note <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A-g_{&lt;&gt;}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\neg</span> A-g_{&lt;&gt;}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> are <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k=f^<span class="pl-c1">0</span>(k)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable by Fact <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{stillstable}(2).  Since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(5K+5)}&gt;<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+4)}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&lt;(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">2</span>)^{4k+4}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, Proposition <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{keylem} implies in case 1 that there exist subgroups <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H_{1}<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> Z_{&lt;&gt;}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H_{0}<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> Z_{&lt;&gt;}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x_{0}, x_{1}<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> Z_{&lt;&gt;}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, such that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H_{1},H_{0}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> have index at most <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>m<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> in <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H_{&lt;&gt;}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and such that </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L666" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="666"></td>

        <td id="LC667" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">|(A-g_{&lt;&gt;})<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (H_{1}+x_{1})|&amp;<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> (1-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4k+4)})|H_{1}|<span class="pl-c1">\text</span>{ and }<span class="pl-c1">\\</span></td>

        <td id="L702" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="702"></td>
        <td id="LC702" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">So assume that for all <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span> <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>^t<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>Z_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is not <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4K+4)}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-excellent.   Fix <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span> <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>^t<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.         <td id="LC717" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">where the last inequalities in each line are because <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f^t(k)<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> K<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.         <td id="L731" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="731"></td>
        <td id="LC731" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> We now show 1-5 holds of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>Z_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta\wedge</span> i}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta\wedge</span> i}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>X_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta\wedge</span> i}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i=<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  It is clear from the above that 1-3 are satisfied.  For (4), we want to show <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>X_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta\wedge</span> i}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f^t(k)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable for each <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">\{</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span>,<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-cce">\}</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  We know that for each <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">\{</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span>,<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-cce">\}</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>N^i(g_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>})<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> X_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f^t(k)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable. By Fact <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{stillstable}(1), <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(N^i(g_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>})<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> X_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>})-x_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta\wedge</span> i}=N^i(g_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}+x_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span> <span class="pl-c1">\wedge</span> i})<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (X_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}-x_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta\wedge</span> i})<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f^t(k)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable.  </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>

        <td id="LC732" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>

        <td id="L733" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="733"></td>
        <td id="LC733" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">We just need to check number 5.  Fix <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>=<span class="pl-c1">\tau\wedge</span> i<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>^{t+1}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  We want to show that for all <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>s<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> t<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span> <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>^s<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span> <span class="pl-c1">\triangleleft</span> <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, the following holds: if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> X_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then</td>

        <td id="LC761" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose this process goes on at least <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> steps.         <td id="LC767" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For each <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span> <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>^d<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, choose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> X_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and set <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}=d_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}+<span class="pl-c1">\sum</span>_{<span class="pl-c1">\sigma\trianglelefteq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}x_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>b_{&lt;&gt;}=g_{&lt;&gt;}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and for each <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span>&lt;s&lt;d<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span> <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>^{s}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>b_{<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span>}= g_{<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span>}+x_{<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span>|_{1}}+<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span> +x_{<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span>|_{s-1}}+x_{<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span>}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Then if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>s&lt;d<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\sigma\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>^s<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>^d<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span> <span class="pl-c1">\trianglelefteq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L768" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="768"></td>
        <td id="LC768" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{align*}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L769" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="769"></td>
        <td id="LC769" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">a_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}+b_{<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span>}&amp;=d_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}+<span class="pl-c1">\sum</span>_{<span class="pl-c1">\tau\trianglelefteq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}x_{<span class="pl-c1">\tau</span>}+g_{<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span>}+x_{<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span>|_{1}}+<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span> +x_{<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span>|_{s-1}}+x_{<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span>}<span class="pl-c1">\\</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L770" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="770"></td>
        <td id="LC770" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">&amp;=d_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}+<span class="pl-c1">\sum</span>_{<span class="pl-c1">\tau\trianglelefteq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}x_{<span class="pl-c1">\tau</span>}+g_{<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span>}+x_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>|_{1}}+<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span> +x_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>|_{s-1}}+x_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>|_s}<span class="pl-c1">\\</span></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L771" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="771"></td>
        <td id="LC771" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">&amp;=d_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}+g_{<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span>}+x_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>|_{s+1}}+<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span> +x_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>|_{d-1}}+x_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}.</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L772" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="772"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L773" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="773"></td>
        <td id="LC773" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> X_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, (<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{5}) implies <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}+b_{<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span>}<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> if and only if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>(s+<span class="pl-c1">1</span>)=<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Thus we have shown that if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span> <span class="pl-c1">\triangleleft</span> <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}b_{<span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span>}<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> E(<span class="pl-c1">\Gamma</span>_A)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> if and only if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\sigma</span> <span class="pl-c1">\wedge</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\trianglelefteq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Recall <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d=d(k)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is as in Fact <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{treefact}.  So since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\Gamma</span>_A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable, the tree bound for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\Gamma</span>_A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is at most <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  However we have just constructed a tree of height <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> in <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\Gamma</span>_A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, a contradiction.  Therefore our inductive construction must end after some <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d&#39;&lt;d<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-steps, meaning we obtain some <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span> <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>^{d&#39;}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H_{<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> of index at most <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>m^{d&#39;}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> which is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{1/(4K+4)}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-excellent.</td>
      </tr>

      <tr>
        <td id="L777" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="777"></td>
        <td id="LC777" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&gt;<span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Then there is a polynomial <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f(x)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> depending only on <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>n<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is sufficiently large the following holds.  If <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> G=<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{Z}/p<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{Z}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable, then there is a subspace <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> of index at most <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>p^{f(1/<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>)}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and a set <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>I<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> G/H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|A<span class="pl-c1">\Delta</span> <span class="pl-c1">\bigcup</span>_{g+H<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> I} g+H|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> |G|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  In other words, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is close to being a union of cosets of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>

      <tr>
        <td id="L780" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="780"></td>
        <td id="LC780" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d=d(k)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> be as in Fact <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{treefact} and set <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>K=f^d(k)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, where <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is as in Fact <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{stillstable}(1).  Set <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>_<span class="pl-c1">0</span>=<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>^{5K+5}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Theorem <span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{mainth} implies there is an <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>_<span class="pl-c1">0</span>^{1/(5K+5)}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-excellent subgroup <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> with index at most <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>p^{d<span class="pl-c1">\lfloor</span> 2/<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>_0<span class="pl-c1">\rfloor</span>}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  By definition of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>_<span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-excellent, and the index of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is at most <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>p^{d<span class="pl-c1">\lfloor</span> 2/<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>_0<span class="pl-c1">\rfloor</span>} <span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> p^{d(2/<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>_0)}=p^{f(1/<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>)}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, where <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>f(x)=<span class="pl-c1">2</span>dx^{5K+5}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>H<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-excellent for <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, we have that for all <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>g<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|(A-g)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> H|=|A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (H+g)|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span> |H|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> or <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|(A-g)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> H|=|A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (H+g)|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> (<span class="pl-c1">1</span>-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>) |H|<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>I=<span class="pl-c1">\{</span>g+H<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G/H: |A<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (H+g)|<span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> (<span class="pl-c1">1</span>-<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>) |H|<span class="pl-cce">\}</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Let </td>

        <td id="LC800" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\section</span>{understanding bohr sets}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L801" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="801"></td>
        <td id="LC801" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L802" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="802"></td>
        <td id="LC802" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B=(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A=B+x<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L803" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="803"></td>
        <td id="LC803" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L804" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="804"></td>
        <td id="LC804" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{lemma}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L805" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="805"></td>
        <td id="LC805" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">If <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&lt;<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">8</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, there is a translate <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B+y<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> disjoint from <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L806" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="806"></td>
        <td id="LC806" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{lemma}</td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L807" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="807"></td>
        <td id="LC807" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{proof}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L808" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="808"></td>
        <td id="LC808" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>N<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> be the maximum order of an element in <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> has order <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>N<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Fix <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\gamma</span> <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> K<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>. Then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-cce">\{</span><span class="pl-c1">\gamma</span>(i x):<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> i<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> N-<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-cce">\}</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is the set of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>N<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-th roots of unity in <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{T}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> (I think...).  Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>z<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> be an <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>N<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-th root of unity such that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|z-<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|&gt;<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>. Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>y=<span class="pl-c1">\gamma</span>^{-1}(z)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Suppose towards a contradiction that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (B+y)<span class="pl-c1">\neq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\emptyset</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Then there is <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> (B+y)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  This means since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\gamma\in</span> K<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\gamma</span>(x)-<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rho</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  On the other hand, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B+y<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> implies <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x-y<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, so <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\gamma</span>(x-y)-<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rho</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\gamma</span>(x)=e^{2<span class="pl-c1">\pi</span> i <span class="pl-c1">\theta</span>}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\gamma</span>(y)=e^{2<span class="pl-c1">\pi</span> i <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Note <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\gamma</span>(x-y)=<span class="pl-c1">\gamma</span>(x)/<span class="pl-c1">\gamma</span>(y)=e^{2<span class="pl-c1">\pi</span> i (<span class="pl-c1">\theta</span> - <span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>)}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Note our assumptions imply <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\gamma</span>(x)-<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|=<span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{2}<span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{1-<span class="pl-c1">\cos</span> (<span class="pl-c1">\theta</span>)}<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rho</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\gamma</span>(y)-<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|=<span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{2}<span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{1-<span class="pl-c1">\cos</span> (<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>)}=|z-<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|&gt;<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/<span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-c1">\geq</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\gamma</span>(x-y)-<span class="pl-c1">1</span>|=<span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{2}<span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{1-<span class="pl-c1">\cos</span> (<span class="pl-c1">\theta</span>-<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>)}<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rho</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  The last inequality implies </td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L809" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="809"></td>
        <td id="LC809" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L810" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="810"></td>
        <td id="LC810" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-c1">1</span>-<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>^<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\cos</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\theta</span>-<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>)=<span class="pl-c1">\cos</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\theta</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\cos</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>)+<span class="pl-c1">\sin</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\theta</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\sin</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>).</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L811" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="811"></td>
        <td id="LC811" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L812" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="812"></td>
        <td id="LC812" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Note <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{2}<span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{1-<span class="pl-c1">\cos</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>)}&gt;<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> implies <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>-<span class="pl-c1">8</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&gt;<span class="pl-c1">\cos</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, which implies <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\cos</span> (<span class="pl-c1">\theta</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\cos</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>)|&lt;<span class="pl-c1">1</span>-<span class="pl-c1">8</span><span class="pl-c1">\eta</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Note <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{2}<span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{1-<span class="pl-c1">\cos</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\theta</span>)}<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rho</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> implies <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>-<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>^<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\cos</span> (<span class="pl-c1">\theta</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, which implies </td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L813" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="813"></td>
        <td id="LC813" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>

        <td id="L814" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="814"></td>
        <td id="LC814" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s">|<span class="pl-c1">\sin</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\theta</span>)|=<span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{1-<span class="pl-c1">\cos</span>^2(<span class="pl-c1">\theta</span>)}<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{1-(1-2<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>^2)^2}=<span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{2}<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span> <span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{1-2<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>^2}&lt;<span class="pl-c1">\sqrt</span>{2}<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&lt;<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span> (<span class="pl-c1">4</span>-<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>),</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L815" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="815"></td>
        <td id="LC815" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L816" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="816"></td>
        <td id="LC816" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">where the last inequality is because <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>&lt;<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Thus <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\sin</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\theta</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\sin</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>)|&lt;<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span> (<span class="pl-c1">4</span>-<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Combining these bounds we obtain that </td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L817" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="817"></td>
        <td id="LC817" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$$</span></span></td>

        <td id="L818" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="818"></td>
        <td id="LC818" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-s">|<span class="pl-c1">\cos</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\theta</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\cos</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>)+<span class="pl-c1">\sin</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\theta</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\sin</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>)|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> |<span class="pl-c1">\cos</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\theta</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\cos</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>)|+|<span class="pl-c1">\sin</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\theta</span>)<span class="pl-c1">\sin</span>(<span class="pl-c1">\eta</span>)|&lt;<span class="pl-c1">1</span>-<span class="pl-c1">8</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span> +<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>(<span class="pl-c1">4</span>-<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>)&lt;<span class="pl-c1">1</span>-<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>^<span class="pl-c1">2</span>,</span></td>

        <td id="LC827" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{lemma}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L828" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="828"></td>
        <td id="LC828" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>G=<span class="pl-c1">\mathbb</span>{Z}/NZ<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> where <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>N<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a large prime number, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a union of translates of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> where <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B=B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\rho</span>)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a regular Bohr set and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span> <span class="pl-c1">\in</span> [?,?]<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Suppose <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(x+B)<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(y+B)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> A=<span class="pl-c1">\emptyset</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>m=<span class="pl-c1">\lfloor</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rho</span> N^{1/|K|}/<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-c1">\rfloor</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  If <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|x-y|&lt;m/k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is not <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>-stable.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L829" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="829"></td>
        <td id="LC829" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{lemma}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L830" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="830"></td>
        <td id="LC830" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{proof}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L831" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="831"></td>
        <td id="LC831" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Because <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is a union of translates of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> which contains some but not all translates of <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, there is a maximal <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> G<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> such that for all <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> y<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> x<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(x+B)<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>

      <tr>
        <td id="L834" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="834"></td>
        <td id="LC834" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">By Lemma 3.3 in &#39;&#39;finite fields ten years on&#39;&#39;, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> contains an arithmetic progression of size at least <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\rho</span> N^{1/|K|}<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> centered at zero. Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>d<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> be the common difference and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>m=<span class="pl-c1">\lfloor</span> <span class="pl-c1">\rho</span> N^{1/|K|}/<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-c1">\rfloor</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, so that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> contains <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>C=<span class="pl-c1">\{</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span>,d,<span class="pl-c1">2</span>d,<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span>, md, -d, -<span class="pl-c1">2</span>d,<span class="pl-c1">\ldots</span>, -md<span class="pl-cce">\}</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>C+x<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> A<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(C+y)<span class="pl-c1">\cap</span> A=<span class="pl-c1">\emptyset</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Without loss assume <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>C+x&lt;C+y<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>x=<span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>=([y/d]d-y)/N<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Since <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>N<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is large, we may assume <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is really small.  Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&#39;<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> [<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>,<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>]<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> be so that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B&#39;=B(K,<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&#39;)<span class="pl-c1">\prec</span>_{<span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&#39;}B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> (<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\epsilon</span>&#39;<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> is still really small).  Then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>B&#39;+B<span class="pl-c1">\approx</span> B<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> (deal with this later), so for now lets assume <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>C+[y/d]d+y<span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> B+y<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, so that we can assume we have some integer <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span><span class="pl-c1">\ell</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> so that <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>C+<span class="pl-c1">\ell</span> d <span class="pl-c1">\subseteq</span> B+y<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, and by assumption <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>|<span class="pl-c1">\ell</span> d-x|=|<span class="pl-c1">\ell</span> d|<span class="pl-c1">\leq</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>+m/k<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L835" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="835"></td>

        <td id="LC836" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Now let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>v_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>=<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>u_<span class="pl-c1">1</span>=<span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  At stage <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>i<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>, let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>v_{i+1}=u_i(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>+<span class="pl-c1">\ell</span>/m)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>u_{i+1}=v_{i+1}+<span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.         <td id="LC838" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Let <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_u=md+md/u<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>b_u=md/u<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  Then <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_u-b_v=md(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>+<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/u-<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/v)<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.  So <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_u-b_v<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> C<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/u-<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/v)<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> [-<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">0</span>]<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> and <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>a_u-b_v<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> C+<span class="pl-c1">\ell</span> d<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span> if <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/u-<span class="pl-c1">1</span>/v)<span class="pl-c1">\in</span> [<span class="pl-c1">\ell</span>/m-<span class="pl-c1">2</span>,<span class="pl-c1">\ell</span>/m]<span class="pl-pds">$</span></span>.</td>
